Connection Closed
Line after Exception </span><span class="token operator" data-token-index="6">-</span><span class="" data-token-index="6"> Method </span><span class="token number" data-token-index="6">1</span><span class="" data-token-index="6">
Line after Exception </span><span class="token operator" data-token-index="6">-</span><span class="" data-token-index="6"> Main

finally block</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="6">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="6">

Finally block is always </span><span class="token function" data-token-index="6">executed</span><span class="" data-token-index="6"> </span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="6">(</span><span class="" data-token-index="6">even when an exception is thrown</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="6">)</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="6">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="6"> So</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="6">,</span><span class="" data-token-index="6"> </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="6">if</span><span class="" data-token-index="6"> we want some code to be
always executed we can move it to finally block</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="6">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="6">

were trying to give quick examples</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> So here is a list </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">of</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> best practices</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">

• Never Hide Exceptions</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> At the least log them</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> printStactTrace method prints the entire stack
trace when an exception occurs</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> If you handle an exception</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">,</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> it is always a good practice to log
the trace</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">

• Do not use exception handling </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">for</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> flow control </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">in</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> a program</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> They have a significant
performance impact</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">

• Think about the user</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> What does the user want to see </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">if</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> there is an exception</span><span class="token operator" data-token-index="0">?</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">

• Think about the support developer</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> What does the support developer need to debug the
exception</span><span class="token operator" data-token-index="0">?</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">

• Think about the calling method</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> Can the calling method </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">do</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> something about the exception being
thrown</span><span class="token operator" data-token-index="0">?</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> If not</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">,</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> create un checked exceptions</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> For example</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">,</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> Spring Framework chooses to make
most </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">of</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> the jdbc exceptions </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">as</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> unchecked exceptions because </span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">,</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">in</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> most cases</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">,</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> there is nothing
that a caller </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">of</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> the method can </span><span class="token keyword" data-token-index="0">do</span><span class="" data-token-index="0"> about a jdbc exception</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span class="" data-token-index="0">

• Have global exception handling</span><span class="token punctuation" data-token-index="0">.</span><span>
